              (bn): BatchNorm2d(384, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.1, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
            )
            (act): ReLU()
            (conv2): Conv_BN(
              (conv): Conv2d(384, 192, kernel_size=(1, 1), stride=(1, 1), bias=False)
              (bn): BatchNorm2d(192, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.1, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
            )
          )
        )
      )
    )
  )
  (subs1): SubSamplingBlock(
    (interact1): ModuleList(
      (0): Residual(
        (f): TokenInteractionBlock(
          (dwconv): Conv_BN(
            (conv): Conv2d(64, 64, kernel_size=(3, 3), stride=(1, 1), padding=(1, 1), groups=64, bias=False)
            (bn): BatchNorm2d(64, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.1, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
          )
        )
      )
    )
    (ffn1): ModuleList(
      (0): Residual(
        (f): FFN(
          (conv1): Conv_BN(
            (conv): Conv2d(64, 128, kernel_size=(1, 1), stride=(1, 1), bias=False)
            (bn): BatchNorm2d(128, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.1, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
          )
          (act): ReLU()
          (conv2): Conv_BN(
            (conv): Conv2d(128, 64, kernel_size=(1, 1), stride=(1, 1), bias=False)
            (bn): BatchNorm2d(64, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.1, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
          )
        )
      )
    )
    (dwconv): InvertedResidualBlock(
      (conv1): Conv_BN(
        (conv): Conv2d(64, 256, kernel_size=(1, 1), stride=(1, 1), bias=False)
        (bn): BatchNorm2d(256, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.1, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
      )
      (act1): ReLU()
      (conv2): Conv_BN(
        (conv): Conv2d(256, 256, kernel_size=(3, 3), stride=(2, 2), padding=(1, 1), groups=256, bias=False)
        (bn): BatchNorm2d(256, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.1, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
      )
      (se): SqueezeExcite(
        (ap): AdaptiveAvgPool2d(output_size=(1, 1))
        (fc1): Conv2d(256, 64, kernel_size=(1, 1), stride=(1, 1))
        (act1): ReLU()
        (fc2): Conv2d(64, 256, kernel_size=(1, 1), stride=(1, 1))
        (act2): Sigmoid()
      )
      (conv3): Conv_BN(
        (conv): Conv2d(256, 128, kernel_size=(1, 1), stride=(1, 1), bias=False)
        (bn): BatchNorm2d(128, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.1, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
      )
    )
    (interact2): ModuleList(
      (0): Residual(
        (f): TokenInteractionBlock(
          (dwconv): Conv_BN(
            (conv): Conv2d(128, 128, kernel_size=(3, 3), stride=(1, 1), padding=(1, 1), groups=128, bias=False)
            (bn): BatchNorm2d(128, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.1, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
          )
        )
      )
    )
    (ffn2): ModuleList(
      (0): Residual(
        (f): FFN(
          (conv1): Conv_BN(
            (conv): Conv2d(128, 256, kernel_size=(1, 1), stride=(1, 1), bias=False)
            (bn): BatchNorm2d(256, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.1, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
          )
          (act): ReLU()
          (conv2): Conv_BN(
            (conv): Conv2d(256, 128, kernel_size=(1, 1), stride=(1, 1), bias=False)
            (bn): BatchNorm2d(128, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.1, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
          )
        )
      )
    )
  )
  (subs2): SubSamplingBlock(
    (interact1): ModuleList(
      (0): Residual(
        (f): TokenInteractionBlock(
          (dwconv): Conv_BN(
            (conv): Conv2d(128, 128, kernel_size=(3, 3), stride=(1, 1), padding=(1, 1), groups=128, bias=False)
            (bn): BatchNorm2d(128, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.1, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
          )
        )
      )
    )
    (ffn1): ModuleList(
      (0): Residual(
        (f): FFN(
          (conv1): Conv_BN(
            (conv): Conv2d(128, 256, kernel_size=(1, 1), stride=(1, 1), bias=False)
            (bn): BatchNorm2d(256, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.1, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
          )
          (act): ReLU()
          (conv2): Conv_BN(
            (conv): Conv2d(256, 128, kernel_size=(1, 1), stride=(1, 1), bias=False)
            (bn): BatchNorm2d(128, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.1, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
          )
        )
      )
    )
    (dwconv): InvertedResidualBlock(
      (conv1): Conv_BN(
        (conv): Conv2d(128, 512, kernel_size=(1, 1), stride=(1, 1), bias=False)
        (bn): BatchNorm2d(512, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.1, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
      )
      (act1): ReLU()
      (conv2): Conv_BN(
        (conv): Conv2d(512, 512, kernel_size=(3, 3), stride=(2, 2), padding=(1, 1), groups=512, bias=False)
        (bn): BatchNorm2d(512, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.1, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
      )
      (se): SqueezeExcite(
        (ap): AdaptiveAvgPool2d(output_size=(1, 1))
        (fc1): Conv2d(512, 128, kernel_size=(1, 1), stride=(1, 1))
        (act1): ReLU()
        (fc2): Conv2d(128, 512, kernel_size=(1, 1), stride=(1, 1))
        (act2): Sigmoid()
      )
      (conv3): Conv_BN(
        (conv): Conv2d(512, 192, kernel_size=(1, 1), stride=(1, 1), bias=False)
        (bn): BatchNorm2d(192, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.1, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
      )
    )
    (interact2): ModuleList(
      (0): Residual(
        (f): TokenInteractionBlock(
          (dwconv): Conv_BN(
            (conv): Conv2d(192, 192, kernel_size=(3, 3), stride=(1, 1), padding=(1, 1), groups=192, bias=False)
            (bn): BatchNorm2d(192, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.1, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
          )
        )
      )
    )
    (ffn2): ModuleList(
      (0): Residual(
        (f): FFN(
          (conv1): Conv_BN(
            (conv): Conv2d(192, 384, kernel_size=(1, 1), stride=(1, 1), bias=False)
            (bn): BatchNorm2d(384, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.1, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
          )
          (act): ReLU()
          (conv2): Conv_BN(
            (conv): Conv2d(384, 192, kernel_size=(1, 1), stride=(1, 1), bias=False)
            (bn): BatchNorm2d(192, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.1, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
          )
        )
      )
    )
  )
  (output): OutputLayer(
    (pool): AdaptiveAvgPool2d(output_size=(1, 1))
    (fc): BN_Linear(
      (bn): BatchNorm1d(192, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.1, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
      (linear): Linear(in_features=192, out_features=100, bias=True)
    )
  )
)
